Young Christian Students Records

University of Notre Dame Archives

Creator: Young Christian Students
Title: Young Christian Students Records
Dates: 1944-1980
Extent: 123 linear feet 5 linear inches of photographs
Language: English.
Identification: YCS

Administrative Information

Related Material

Return to the Table of Contents

Background

A movement of the lay apostolate involving students in Catholic Action: a national organization, with international affiliations, consisting of local cells of student leaders who meet to observe, judge, and act in accordance with the principles of Canon Joseph Cardijn, founder of the European Jocist movement.

Return to the Table of Contents

Scope and Content

Correspondence (1958-1965); reports from local leaders (1960-1965); records of national committee meetings (1956-1964); records of summer training sessions and national and regional study weeks (1944-1966); files on recruitment, training, and activities of full-time YCS workers (1947-1967); records of staff meetings at national headquarters (1957-1965); financial files, subject files, research files, photographs, reports, programs, bulletins, handbooks, and other publications; with information on YCS chaplains and the YCS at all levels--college, high school, and grade school; and records of the Chicago-area YCS (1968-1980), including correspondence, financial records, subject files, and printed material;

Return to the Table of Contents

Return to the Table of Contents

CYCS III Committee Meetings

The National Committee of the YCS consisted of the National Staff, (outgoing staffers attended, along with their replacements) and the area representatives or their substitutes. Observers also attended. Meetings were held in June and December. The records of the 1957-1964 meetings, including many detailed reports, are in boxes 2 and 3.

In 1963, a new "joint" committee for coordinating activity, composed of two priests, five students,and three staff members, (these numbers fluctuated at later at later meetings) was formed to discuss problems of programming, expansion, and finances. The first of the bi-annual meetings was held September 5, 1963. The records of this committee to 1966 including agendas, minutes, reports and correspondence are in box 3. Box 138 contains copies of some of the mimeographed material generated by these committees, mainly copies of the minutes of the joint committee meetings.

CYCS IV Summer Sessions

The YCS headquarters sponsored summer training courses for small groups (ca. 20) of students from throughout the country. Similar sessions of varying length were occasionally held in other sections of the country.

CYCS V Study Weeks and Meetings - Regional and National

The national and regional study weeks complemented the Summer Sessions by reaching larger numbers of Young Christian Students. Between 100 and 200 students attended these national conventions which were held in the midwest in June. The study weeks featured speakers, panel discussions, and workshops. The files for the National Study Weeks are quite complete, with correspondence, agendas, and copies; regional study week files are much less complete. The earliest material dates from the 1940s.

CYCS XI North American Regional Federation

Series eleven contains similar material to series ten, but limited to the North American region. Representatives of the national YCS movements in this area kept in close contact, and held annual meetings, usually in Canada. The Canadian and U.S. YCS federations were by far the most active,but there was contact with Caribbean area YCS groups.
